    const IMG_SEL = 'img.responsive-img_img';
    const isIphone = (window.navigator.userAgent.match('iPhone'));

    const io = window.IntersectionObserver && new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
        entries.filter(entry => entry.isIntersecting).forEach(entry => io.unobserve(entry.target));
    }, {
        rootMargin: '0px'
    });

    if (isIphone) {
        document.querySelectorAll(IMG_SEL)?.forEach((img) => {
            const imageSize = img?.parentElement?.getAttribute('data-desiredImageSize');
            if (img.clientWidth && imageSize !== 'marketing_promo_image') {
                img.sizes = img.clientWidth + 'px';
            }
            io?.observe(img);
        });
    } else {
        document.querySelectorAll(IMG_SEL)?.forEach((img) => {
